\nwnotused{GFF\ DATA\ STRUCTURE}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{456}\nwdocspar
\end{comment}%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{457}\sublabel{NWgff18-ParI-E}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ParI-E}}}\moddef{Parsing Input Data~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ParI-1}}}\plusendmoddef
sub add_gff_record() \{
    my $_gff = $_[0];
    \LA{}add align records to aplot DS~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-addT-1}}\RA{}
    my ($VarName,$Counter,$Type);
    ($VarName,$Counter,$Type) = (
        \\%GFF_DATA,
        \\$seq_COUNT,
        'SEQUENCE' );
    &load_gff_var($seqname,$VarName,$Counter,$Type);
    ($VarName,$Counter,$Type) = (
        \\%\{$VarName->\{$seqname\}[$_element]\},
        \\$$VarName\{$seqname\}[$_counter][$_elemNum],
        'SOURCE' );
    &load_gff_var($source,$VarName,$Counter,$Type);
    ($VarName,$Counter,$Type) = ( 
        \\%\{$VarName->\{$source\}[$_element]\},
        \\$$VarName\{$source\}[$_counter][$_elemNum],
        'STRAND' );
    &load_gff_var($strand,$VarName,$Counter,$Type);
    ($VarName,$Counter,$Type) = (
        \\%\{$VarName->\{$strand\}[$_element]\},
        \\$$VarName\{$strand\}[$_counter][$_elemNum],
        'GROUP' );
    &load_gff_var($group,$VarName,$Counter,$Type);
    \LA{}adding new feature elements~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-addR-1}}\RA{}
    return;
\} # add_gff_record
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{458}\nwdocspar

First we load the plain GFF attributes for a given record, when such record is defining a vector we add a new element to the feature anonymous array. That element is a list of the scores provided by the '{\tt{}{\char38}load{\char95}GFF{\char95}vector}' function defined in section~\ref{sec:loadvector}, page~\pageref{sec:loadvector}.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{459}\sublabel{NWgff18-addR-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-addR-1}}}\moddef{adding new feature elements~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-addR-1}}}\endmoddef
push @\{$VarName->\{$group\}[$_element]\},
    [
      'G',      # Type == plain GFF
      \{\},       # Properties hash, now empty
      $feature, # GFF feature (3rd field)
      $label,   # Record ID if exist, order# otherwise
      $start,
      $end,
      $score,
      $frame,
    ];
my $t = ++$VarName->\{$group\}[$_counter][$_elemNum];
&set_var_defaults('FEATURE',
                  \\%\{$VarName->\{$group\}[$_element][($t-1)][$_prop]\});
$_gff eq $VECTOR && do \{
    @\{$VarName->\{$group\}[$_element][8]\} = [ @vect_ary ];
\};
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-ParI-E}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{460}\nwdocspar

If the standard GFF alignment format is found, we process them as if it was an aplot records, so that we have to set all the variables required to fill such data structure ('{\tt{}{\char37}ALN{\char95}DATA}' in section~\ref{sec:APLOT-DS} , page~\pageref{sec:APLOT-DS}).

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{461}\sublabel{NWgff18-addT-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-addT-1}}}\moddef{add align records to aplot DS~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-addT-1}}}\endmoddef
$_gff eq $ALIGN && do \{
    &add_aplot_record;
    return;
\};
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-ParI-E}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{462}\nwdocspar

We declare here the main variable containing all the GFF data, and auxiliary variables containing the array indexes used in the anonymous arrays defined within that variable.\label{sec:GFF-DS}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{463}\sublabel{NWgff18-GloB-B}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-B}}}\moddef{Global Vars~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-1}}}\plusendmoddef
my (%GFF_DATA,$seq_COUNT);
my ($_counter,$_prop,$_element) = (0,1,2);
my ($_order,$_elemNum,$_ori,$_end) = (0,1,2,4);
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{464}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{465}\sublabel{NWgff18-ParI-F}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ParI-F}}}\moddef{Parsing Input Data~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ParI-1}}}\plusendmoddef
sub load_gff_var() \{
    my ($_value,$_var,$_cnt,$_type) = @_;
    defined($$_var\{$_value\}) || do \{
        $$_var\{$_value\}[$_counter] = [ ++$$_cnt, 0, 0, 0 ];
        &set_var_defaults($_type,\\%\{$$_var\{$_value\}[$_prop]\});
    \};
    return;
\} # load_gff_var
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{466}%$

We initialize properties for each new element as references to '{\tt{}{\char37}DefaultVars}' given level corresponding values. 

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{467}\sublabel{NWgff18-ParI-G}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ParI-G}}}\moddef{Parsing Input Data~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ParI-1}}}\plusendmoddef
sub set_var_defaults() \{
    my ($sect,$varhash) = @_;
    foreach my $nm (keys %\{$DefaultVars\{$sect\}\}) \{
        $$varhash\{$nm\} = \\$DefaultVars\{$sect\}\{$nm\}\{'VALUE'\};
    \};
    return;
\} # load_gff_var
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{468}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{Parsing grouping attributes}

'{\tt{}GFF{\char95}CHOICE}' block sets some variables depending on the record format, standard GFF or APLOT GFF-like. Once we have the attribute string from the GFF/APLOT record, we first check if it is empty, then we split by semicolons which will have or not white spaces or tabs before and/or after, as shown in this regular expression:\\
\centerline{'{\tt{}/{\char92}b{\char92}s*;{\char92}s*{\char92}b/}'}\\
This will define tag-value pairs (and maybe some extra fields).  

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{469}\sublabel{NWgff18-ParI-H}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ParI-H}}}\moddef{Parsing Input Data~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ParI-1}}}\plusendmoddef
sub load_grouping() \{
    my ($_type,$attributes) = @_;
    my ($grp_string,$grp_counter,$grp_GP,$grp_NOGP,$grp_tag);
  GFF_CHOICE: \{
    $_type && do \{ 
        $grp_string = "$seqname\\_$source\\_$strand";
        $grp_counter = ++$group_gff_counter;
        $grp_GP = $GFF;
        $grp_NOGP = $GFF_NOGP;
        $grp_tag = '';
        last GFF_CHOICE;
    \};
    $grp_string = "$seqname_1\\_$seqname_2\\_$source_1\\_$strand_1$strand_2";
    $grp_counter = ++$group_aplot_counter;
    $grp_GP = $APLOT;
    $grp_NOGP = $APLOT_NOGP;
    $grp_tag = $SOURCE\{'align_tag'\}; # %SOURCE is a temporary hash name
  \};
    $label = $group_id = $grp_counter;
    defined($attributes) || do \{
        $group = "$grp_string\\_$group_id";
        return $grp_NOGP;
    \};
    my @grouping_list = ();
    @grouping_list = split /\\b\\s*;\\s*\\b/o, $attributes;
    \LA{}parse grouping attributes~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-parP-1}}\RA{}
    \LA{}parse other attributes~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-parM-1}}\RA{}
    return $grp_GP;
\}
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{470}\nwdocspar

We may find four basic grouping field structures (detailed in Table~\ref{tbl:formats}) within the first element of '{\tt{}@grouping{\char95}list}'. We check first for double-quotes in the first or second field within that element. If second field is double-quoted, the first field is set as 'Tag' and the quoted as 'Value', else 'Tag' is set to default value (empty string for GFF records and 'target' for APLOT GFF-like ones) and 'Value' is set with the first field. Then we are looking in GFF grouping attributes for extra fields defining start, end, strand and frame (all related to the second sequence); in APLOT GFF-like format, those values are deprecated (because they must be defined in the first eight fields following the first sequence values and a colon as shown in table~\ref{tbl:formats}). 

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{471}\sublabel{NWgff18-parP-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-parP-1}}}\moddef{parse grouping attributes~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-parP-1}}}\endmoddef
my $grp_flag = 0;
my @new_group = ();
my $groupregexp = '^(.*?)(?:"(.+?)"(?:\\s+\\b(.*))?)?$'; #'
my $group_string = shift @grouping_list;
($group_string =~ /$groupregexp/o) && 
    (@new_group = ($1,$2,$3));
$new_group[0] =~ s/\\b\\s*$//o;
$new_group[0] || do \{  # type 2 attributes
    $grp_flag = 1;
    $new_group[0] = $grp_tag;
\};
$new_group[1] || do \{  # type 1 attributes
    $grp_flag = 1;
    $new_group[1] = $new_group[0];
    $new_group[0] = $grp_tag;
\};
($tag,$group) = (lc($new_group[0]),$new_group[1]);
# Here looking for colon field separator in aplot GFF-like grouping
($grp_flag && $group =~ /^(.*?):(.*?)$/o) && (($group,$label) = ($1,$2));
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-ParI-H}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{472}%$

Here we look for other attribute fields, those defining coords for the target sequence match in standard GFF format and those defining a scoring vector, both formats are explained more in detail in the following two subsections.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{473}\sublabel{NWgff18-parM-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-parM-1}}}\moddef{parse other attributes~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-parM-1}}}\endmoddef
$_type && do \{ # GFF grouping
    $tag =~ /$SOURCE\{'align_tag'\}/ && do \{
        &load_GFF_align;
        return $ALIGN;
    \}; 
    $tag =~ /$SOURCE\{'vector_tag'\}/ && do \{
        &load_GFF_vector;
        return $VECTOR;
    \};
\};
\nwalsodefined{\\{NWgff18-parM-2}}\nwused{\\{NWgff18-ParI-H}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{474}\nwdocspar

We are interested in finding 'id' tag, that defines the label for a single record, this is implemented in the '{\tt{}{\char38}load{\char95}GFF{\char95}align}' and '{\tt{}{\char38}load{\char95}GFF{\char95}vector}'functions but has to be parsed in plain GFF records.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{475}\sublabel{NWgff18-parM-2}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-parM-2}}}\moddef{parse other attributes~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-parM-1}}}\plusendmoddef
scalar(@grouping_list) > 0 && do\{ 
    foreach my $element (@grouping_list) \{
        ($element =~ /$groupregexp/o) && (@new_group = ($1,$2,$3));
        lc($new_group[0]) =~ $SOURCE\{'label_tag'\} && do \{
            $label = $new_group[1];
            $label eq "" && do \{
                (undef,$label,undef) = split /\\s+/og, $new_group[0];
            \};
        \};
    \};
\};
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{476}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{477}\sublabel{NWgff18-defQ-2}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-defQ-2}}}\moddef{default layout vars values~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-defQ-1}}}\plusendmoddef
align_tag                  => \{ TYPE => 'STRING' , VALUE => 'target' \},
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{478}\nwdocspar
\begin{comment}
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{479}\sublabel{NWgff18-cusN-2}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cusN-2}}}\moddef{custom-vars latex short~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cusN-1}}}\plusendmoddef
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{480}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{481}\sublabel{NWgff18-cusH-2}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cusH-2}}}\moddef{custom-vars latex~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cusH-1}}}\plusendmoddef
\\vnlitem\{align\\_tag\}\{string\}\{Target\} \\tp\{align\\_tag\} holds the specific tag (for a grouping Tag-Value pair) to detect those GFF records coding for alignment data and having the following group structure:\\\\[1ex]
\\centerline\{\\shortstack[r]\{align\\_tag "group\\_name" \\pr\{seq2\\_start\} \\pr\{seq2\\_end\} [ ; Strand \\pr\{seq2\\_strand\} \\eoline\\\\\\,[ ; Frame \\pr\{seq2\\_frame\} [ ; E\\_value \\pr\{score\} ]\\,]\\,]\\hspace\{3ex\}\}\}\\\\[0.75ex]
so the program can recover the coords for the target sequence from the grouping fields. Remember that tags are not case-sensitive. 
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{482}\nwdocspar
\end{comment}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{483}\sublabel{NWgff18-defQ-3}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-defQ-3}}}\moddef{default layout vars values~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-defQ-1}}}\plusendmoddef
vector_tag                 => \{ TYPE => 'STRING' , VALUE => 'vector' \},
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{484}\nwdocspar
\begin{comment}
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{485}\sublabel{NWgff18-cusN-3}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cusN-3}}}\moddef{custom-vars latex short~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cusN-1}}}\plusendmoddef
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{486}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{487}\sublabel{NWgff18-cusH-3}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cusH-3}}}\moddef{custom-vars latex~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cusH-1}}}\plusendmoddef
\\vnlitem\{vector\\_tag\}\{string\}\{Vector\} \\tp\{vector\\_tag\} sets the specific tag (for a grouping Tag-Value pair) to detect scoring vector GFF records, which have the following group structure:\\\\[1ex]
\\centerline\{\\shortstack[r]\{vector\\_tag "group\\_name" \\pr\{vector\\_type\} [ ; Window \\pr\{window\\_length\} \\eoline\\\\\\, [ ; Step \\pr\{step\\_length\} ]\\,] ; Scores \\pr\{score$_0$\} ... \\pr\{score$_n$\}\\hspace\{3ex\}\}\}\\\\[0.75ex]
so the program can parse the list of single scores from the grouping fields. Remember that tags are not case-sensitive.
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{488}\nwdocspar
\end{comment}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{489}\sublabel{NWgff18-defQ-4}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-defQ-4}}}\moddef{default layout vars values~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-defQ-1}}}\plusendmoddef
label_tag                  => \{ TYPE => 'STRING' , VALUE => 'id'   \},
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{490}\nwdocspar
\begin{comment}
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{491}\sublabel{NWgff18-cusN-4}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cusN-4}}}\moddef{custom-vars latex short~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cusN-1}}}\plusendmoddef
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{492}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{493}\sublabel{NWgff18-cusH-4}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cusH-4}}}\moddef{custom-vars latex~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cusH-1}}}\plusendmoddef
\\vnlitem\{label\\_tag\}\{string\}\{Id\} \\tp\{label\\_tag\} sets the specific tag (for a grouping Tag-Value pair) that allows to identify a single record. The program looks for the grouping Tag-Value pair for which the tag matches \\tp\{label\\_tag\} and takes \\tp\{value\} as the specific record label. You must have an attribute like this within the grouping attribute list:\\\\[0.75ex]
\\centerline\{\\ldots ; label\\_tag "element\\_label" [ ; \\ldots \}\\\\[0.5ex]
Using this attribute makes easy to set specific properties for one or more elements. Remember that tags are not case-sensitive.
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{494}\nwdocspar
\end{comment}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{495}\sublabel{NWgff18-GloB-C}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-C}}}\moddef{Global Vars~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-1}}}\plusendmoddef
my %SOURCE = ( # this is a temporary hash name (to implement later)
               align_tag  => 'target',
               vector_tag => 'vector',
               label_tag  => 'id',
               );
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{496}\nwdocspar

% \subsctn{Parsing extended GFF format}\label{sec:parseXTRA}

The following record formats share the field structure of a GFF standard record, but there are special tags in the grouping fields containing data that will be used by {\prog}. Both formats require a fixed tag string (by default 'Vector' for the scoring vectors and 'Target' for the alignment data), which can be defined by users with the variable '{\tt{}{\char37}SOURCE}' \textbf{(provisional varname)}.

sub ps_header() \{
    print STDOUT << "+++HEADER+++";
%!PS-Adobe-3.0
%%Title: title
%%Creator: $PROGRAM
%%Version: $VERSION
%%CreationDate: $DATE
%%For: $USER
%%Pages: 1
%%Orientation: Portrait
%%BoundingBox: 0 0 595 842
%%EndComments
%
\LA{}GNU License PostScript~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GNUM-1}}\RA{}
%
% $LAST_UPDATE
%
% Report BUGS to: jabril@\\imim.es 
%
%%BeginProlog
%
\LA{}POSTSCRIPT shortnames~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSL-1}}\RA{}
\LA{}POSTSCRIPT constants~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSK-1}}\RA{}
+++HEADER+++
\} # ps_header

\subsctn{CMYK color definition}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{515}\sublabel{NWgff18-PosH.2-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PosH.2-1}}}\moddef{PostScript COLORS~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PosH.2-1}}}\endmoddef
sub ps_colors() \{
  my %tmp = ();
  print STDOUT "%% Fixed Color Variables (CMYK)\\n";
  print STDOUT "/colordict ".($colors + 28)." dict def colordict begin %% ".
               $colors." colors + 28 definitions\\n";
  foreach my $key (keys %COLORS) \{ $tmp\{$COLORS\{$key\}->[0]\} = $key \};
  for (my $j = 1; $j <= $colors; $j++) \{ 
      my $name = $tmp\{$j\};
      my $ref = \\$COLORS\{$name\};
      my $cmyk = "$$ref->[1] $$ref->[2] $$ref->[3] $$ref->[4]";
      print STDOUT "/".(&fill_right($name,20," "))."\{ $cmyk \} def\\n";
      \};
  print STDOUT "end %% colordict\\n";
\} # ps_colors
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-PosM-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{516}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{517}\sublabel{NWgff18-GloB-E}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-E}}}\moddef{Global Vars~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-1}}}\plusendmoddef
my $colors = 0;
my %COLORS = (    # [ ColorNUMBER, qw/ CYAN MAGENTA YELLOW BLACK / ]
  \LA{}cmyk colors perl definition~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cmyR-1}}\RA{}
  ); # %COLORS
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{518}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{Page formats definition}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{519}\sublabel{NWgff18-PosI-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PosI-1}}}\moddef{PostScript FORMATS~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PosI-1}}}\endmoddef
sub ps_page_formats() \{
  my %tmp = ();
  print STDOUT "%% Paper Sizes (in points)\\n";
  print STDOUT "/pagedict ".($formats + 2)." dict def pagedict begin %% ".
               $formats." formats + 2 definitions\\n";
  foreach my $key (keys %FORMATS) \{ $tmp\{$FORMATS\{$key\}->[0]\} = $key \};
  for (my $j = 1; $j <= $formats; $j++) \{ 
      my $name = $tmp\{$j\};
      my $ref = \\$FORMATS\{$name\};
      my $pgsz = &fill_left($$ref->[1],4," ").&fill_left($$ref->[2],5," ");
      print STDOUT "/pg".(&fill_right($name,10," "))."\{ $pgsz \} def\\n";
      \};
  print STDOUT "end %% pagedict\\n";\}
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-PosM-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{520}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{521}\sublabel{NWgff18-GloB-F}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-F}}}\moddef{Global Vars~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-1}}}\plusendmoddef
my $formats = 0;
my %FORMATS = (   # [ FormatNUMBER, X(short edge), Y(long edge) ]
  \LA{}page sizes perl definition~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-pagQ-1}}\RA{}
  );
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{522}\nwdocspar

\LA{}POSTSCRIPT layout~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSH-1}}\RA{}

\LA{}POSTSCRIPT aplotdict~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSK.2-1}}\RA{}

0.125 setlinewidth

\subsctn{{\ps} code chunks}

\subsubsctn{Page boundaries}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{527}\sublabel{NWgff18-PosK-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PosK-1}}}\moddef{Postscript OPEN PAGE~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PosK-1}}}\endmoddef
sub ps_open_page() \{
    print STDOUT << '+++OPEN+++';
%%Page: 1 1
%%BeginPageSetup
%
% Saving current page settings
/pgsave save def
% Setting BGcolor for sheet
Dpage 0 0 bbox S BGcolor scmyk fill R clip newpath
% Setting page-size scale
1 CSF dup F
%%EndPageSetup
%
+++OPEN+++
\} # ps_open_page
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-PosM-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{528}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{529}\sublabel{NWgff18-PosL-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PosL-1}}}\moddef{Postscript CLOSE PAGE~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PosL-1}}}\endmoddef
sub ps_close_page() \{
    print STDOUT << '+++CLOSE+++';
%
flgcrd \{ s_credits \} if
grestoreall
pgsave restore
showpage
%
%%PageEND: 1 1
%
+++CLOSE+++
\} # ps_close_page
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-PosM-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{530}\nwdocspar

\sctn{CMYK color definition} %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
\label{sec:CMYKcolordef}

To avoid mistakes when working with three separate files, we define here CMYK color names used by this perl program, their {\LaTeX} definition ('{\tt{}AplotColorDefs.tex}') and the table sumarizing them for the manual ('{\tt{}AplotColorTbl.tex}'). % outlined in page~\pageref{sec:cmykfiles}.

\subsctn{Black and White}

\newcommand{\clrtbl}[5]{\vskip -2.5ex \noindent\hrulefill\cln{#1}\cln{#2}\cln{#3}\cln{#4}\cln{#5}}
\newcommand{\clrtblg}[7]{\vskip -2.5ex \noindent\hrulefill\cln{#1}\cln{#2}\cln{#3}\cln{#4}\cln{#5}\cln{#6}\cln{#7}}

\clrtblg{black}{verydarkgrey}{darkgrey}{grey}{lightgrey}{verylightgrey}{white}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{533}\sublabel{NWgff18-cmyR-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cmyR-1}}}\moddef{cmyk colors perl definition~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cmyR-1}}}\endmoddef
# black+grey+white
black              => [ ++$colors, qw/ 0.00 0.00 0.00 1.00 / ],
verydarkgrey       => [ ++$colors, qw/ 0.00 0.00 0.00 0.80 / ],
darkgrey           => [ ++$colors, qw/ 0.00 0.00 0.00 0.60 / ],
grey               => [ ++$colors, qw/ 0.00 0.00 0.00 0.40 / ],
lightgrey          => [ ++$colors, qw/ 0.00 0.00 0.00 0.20 / ],
verylightgrey      => [ ++$colors, qw/ 0.00 0.00 0.00 0.10 / ],
white              => [ ++$colors, qw/ 0.00 0.00 0.00 0.00 / ],
\nwalsodefined{\\{NWgff18-cmyR-2}\\{NWgff18-cmyR-3}\\{NWgff18-cmyR-4}\\{NWgff18-cmyR-5}\\{NWgff18-cmyR-6}\\{NWgff18-cmyR-7}\\{NWgff18-cmyR-8}\\{NWgff18-cmyR-9}\\{NWgff18-cmyR-A}\\{NWgff18-cmyR-B}\\{NWgff18-cmyR-C}\\{NWgff18-cmyR-D}}\nwused{\\{NWgff18-GloB-E}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{534}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{535}\sublabel{NWgff18-cmyS-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cmyS-1}}}\moddef{cmyk colors latex definition~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cmyS-1}}}\endmoddef
% black+grey+white
\\definecolor\{black\}              \{cmyk\}\{0.00,0.00,0.00,1.00\}
\\definecolor\{verydarkgrey\}       \{cmyk\}\{0.00,0.00,0.00,0.80\}
\\definecolor\{darkgrey\}           \{cmyk\}\{0.00,0.00,0.00,0.60\}
\\definecolor\{grey\}               \{cmyk\}\{0.00,0.00,0.00,0.40\}
\\definecolor\{lightgrey\}          \{cmyk\}\{0.00,0.00,0.00,0.20\}
\\definecolor\{verylightgrey\}      \{cmyk\}\{0.00,0.00,0.00,0.10\}
\\definecolor\{white\}              \{cmyk\}\{0.00,0.00,0.00,0.00\}
\nwalsodefined{\\{NWgff18-cmyS-2}\\{NWgff18-cmyS-3}\\{NWgff18-cmyS-4}\\{NWgff18-cmyS-5}\\{NWgff18-cmyS-6}\\{NWgff18-cmyS-7}\\{NWgff18-cmyS-8}\\{NWgff18-cmyS-9}\\{NWgff18-cmyS-A}\\{NWgff18-cmyS-B}\\{NWgff18-cmyS-C}\\{NWgff18-cmyS-D}}\nwused{\\{NWgff18-LATH.2-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{536}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{537}\sublabel{NWgff18-cmyN-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cmyN-1}}}\moddef{cmyk color table - left~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-cmyN-1}}}\endmoddef
% black+grey+white
\\clspc
\\clrow\{black\}                    & 0.00 & 0.00 & 0.00 & 1.00 \\\\
\\clrow\{verydarkgrey\}             & 0.00 & 0.00 & 0.00 & 0.80 \\\\
\\clrow\{darkgrey\}                 & 0.00 & 0.00 & 0.00 & 0.60 \\\\
\\clrow\{grey\}                     & 0.00 & 0.00 & 0.00 & 0.40 \\\\
\\clrow\{lightgrey\}                & 0.00 & 0.00 & 0.00 & 0.20 \\\\

\\definecolor\{orange\}             \{cmyk\}\{0.00,0.30,0.80,0.00\}

\subsctn{Colors Help}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{611}\sublabel{NWgff18-colB-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-colB-1}}}\moddef{colors help~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-colB-1}}}\endmoddef
Those are the colors defined in $PROGRAM:
+ Basic Colors: black white.
+ Variable Colors: 
      grey magenta violet blue skyblue cyan seagreen
         green limegreen yellow orange red brown
  You can get five color shades from Variable Colors with
  \\"verydark\\", \\"dark\\", \\"light\\" and \\"verylight\\" prefixes,
  as example: 
    verydarkblue, darkblue, blue, lightblue and verylightblue.
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-MaiD-2}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{612}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{Page sizes help}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{625}\sublabel{NWgff18-pagA-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-pagA-1}}}\moddef{pages help~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-pagA-1}}}\endmoddef
The following page sizes are available: from A0 to A10, 
from B0 to B10, 10x14, executive, folio, ledger, legal, 
letter, quarto, statement and tabloid.

\sctn{{\ps} main program and routines} %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\subsctn{Abbreviated function names}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{627}\sublabel{NWgff18-POSL-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSL-1}}}\moddef{POSTSCRIPT shortnames~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSL-1}}}\endmoddef
%%BeginProcSet: Short_names 1.0 0
%
/tflg false def % test flag
/bdf \{ bind def \} bind def
/xdf \{ exch def \} bdf
/cm \{ 28.35 mul \} bdf
/ivcm \{ 28.35 div \} bdf
/in \{ 72    mul \} bdf
/F \{ scale \} bdf
/T \{ translate \} bdf
/S \{ gsave \} bdf
/R \{ grestore \} bdf
/m \{ moveto \} bdf
/rm \{ rmoveto \} bdf
/l \{ lineto \} bdf
/rl \{ rlineto \} bdf
/K \{ stroke \} bdf
/scmyk \{ setcmykcolor \} bdf
/slw \{ setlinewidth \} bdf
/bbox \{ 4 copy 3 1 roll exch 6 2 roll 8 -2 roll m l l l closepath \} bdf
/dotted \{ [ 1 ] 0 setdash \} def
%
%%EndProcSet:   Short_names 1.0 0
%

\subsctn{Defining PS constants}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{629}\sublabel{NWgff18-POSK-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSK-1}}}\moddef{POSTSCRIPT constants~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSK-1}}}\endmoddef
%%BeginProcSet: Constants 1.0 0
%
% Printing Offset
/VUpOS 0.25 cm def  % offset defines non printable
/VDnOS 0.25 cm def  % paper area for pages (printer outlimits).
/HLtOS 0.25 cm def
/HRtOS 0.25 cm def
/htag   0 def
/Xmarg  5.0 cm def       % Starting Point (upper left corner)
/Ymarg  842 2 cm sub def
/Y Ymarg def
/PlotWidth  14 cm def    % Blocks Size
/Spacer   1.00 cm def    % BBox relative to dotplot
/BBoxX  PlotWidth def    % SBox relative to percent box
/BBoxY   14.00 cm def    % XBox relative to extra box
/SBoxX  PlotWidth def
/SBoxY    2.25 cm def
/XBoxX  PlotWidth def
/XBoxY    3.00 cm def
/WBox     0.50 cm def    % TagBox Size
/HWBox WBox 2 div    def
/Warw  WBox 0.75 mul def
/HWarw Warw 2 div    def
%
%%EndProcSet:   Constants 1.0 0
%
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-PosH-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{630}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{Page layout}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{631}\sublabel{NWgff18-POSH-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSH-1}}}\moddef{POSTSCRIPT layout~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSH-1}}}\endmoddef
%%BeginProcSet: Page_Layout 1.0 0
%
/TitleFont    \{ 24 /Times-Bold  \} def
/SubTtFont    \{ 16 /Times-Roman \} def
/ElmFont      \{ 12 FTLbsc mul /Times-Roman \} def
/TagFont      \{ 14 GPLbsc mul /Times-Roman \} def
/TagLabelFont \{ 16 /Times-Bold  \} def
/TickFont     \{ 10 /Helvetica \} def
%
/xBDspl  1.8 putExon add putExLbl add putGnLbl add def % 1.25
/xGLDspl 1.0 putExon add putExLbl add def              % 0.85
/xGDspl  0.75 putExon add putExLbl add def
/FBDspl 0.60 def % For example, for mRNA.
%
/vertical   \{ /htag 0 def \} bdf
/horizontal \{ /htag 1 def \} bdf
%
/FSF 4 def % Point size for Credits for A4
/CSF \{ pagedict begin pga4 pop end Dpage pop exch div mul \} bdf
%
% checking if margins are within the defined offset
flglscape \{
 UpM HLtOS lt \{ /UpM HLtOS def \} if % Checking margins for flglscape mode
 DnM HRtOS lt \{ /DnM HRtOS def \} if
 LtM VDnOS lt \{ /LtM VDnOS def \} if
 RtM VUpOS lt \{ /RtM VUpOS def \} if
 \} \{
  UpM VUpOS lt \{ /UpM VUpOS def \} if % Checking margins for portrait mode
  DnM VDnOS lt \{ /DnM VDnOS def \} if
  LtM HLtOS lt \{ /LtM HLtOS def \} if
  RtM HRtOS lt \{ /RtM HRtOS def \} if
  \} ifelse
% defining pagelimits and X - Y scales (Xlim Ylim)
/pglim \{ Dpage pop LtM RtM add sub Dpage exch pop UpM DnM add sub \} def
% Defining starting point on page.
/XORI LtM def
/YORI UpM def
%
%%EndProcSet:   Page_Layout 1.0 0
%
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-PosF.3-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{632}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{Text related functions}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{633}\sublabel{NWgff18-POSP-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSP-1}}}\moddef{POSTSCRIPT text functions~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSP-1}}}\endmoddef
%%BeginProcSet: text_functions 1.0 0
%
/sfont \{ findfont exch scalefont setfont \} bdf
/tshow \{ S scmyk sfont m rotate show R \} bdf
/ctshow \{
  10 -1 roll dup 11 1 roll 7 -2 roll 2 copy 9 2 roll 
  S sfont stringwidth pop R 2 div 
  htag 1 eq \{
    9 -1 roll exch sub 8 1 roll
    \} \{
      8 -1 roll exch sub 7 1 roll
    \} ifelse
  tshow
  \} bdf
/ltshow \{
  10 -1 roll dup 11 1 roll 7 -2 roll 2 copy 9 2 roll 
  S sfont stringwidth pop R 
  htag 1 eq \{
    9 -1 roll exch sub 8 1 roll
    \} \{
      8 -1 roll exch sub 7 1 roll
    \} ifelse
  tshow
  \} bdf
%
% X Y angle string valign halign fnt color ttxt
 % valign : tv (top)  cv (middle) bv (bottom)
 % halign : lh (left) ch (center) rh (right)
/chrh \{ 
  S newpath 0 0 m false 
  charpath flattenpath pathbbox exch pop
  3 -1 roll pop R
  \} bdf
/strh \{
  2 dict begin /lly 0.0 def /ury 0.0 def 
  \{ ( ) dup 0 4 -1 roll put chrh 
    dup ury gt \{ /ury xdf \} \{ pop \} ifelse
    dup lly lt \{ /lly xdf \} \{ pop \} ifelse
    \} forall
  ury end
  \} bdf
/ttxt \{
  S scmyk sfont 8 dict begin 
  /h xdf /v xdf /lbl xdf /angle xdf /y xdf /x xdf 
  /hs lbl stringwidth pop neg def /vs lbl strh neg def
  x y T angle rotate
  h (rh) eq \{ hs
    \} \{
      h (ch) eq \{ hs 2 div \} \{ 0 \} ifelse
    \} ifelse
  v (tv) eq \{ vs
    \} \{
      v (cv) eq \{ vs 2 div \} \{ 0 \} ifelse
    \} ifelse
  m lbl show end R
  \} bdf
%
/Title \{ S 0 Xmarg Y TitleFont FGcolor tshow R /Y Y 0.75 cm sub def \} bdf 
/SubTitle \{ S 0 Xmarg Y SubTtFont FGcolor tshow R /Y Y 2.5 cm sub def \} bdf 
%
%%EndProcSet:   text_functions 1.0 0
%
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-PosF.3-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{634}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{The APLOT dictionary}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{635}\sublabel{NWgff18-POSK.2-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSK.2-1}}}\moddef{POSTSCRIPT aplotdict~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSK.2-1}}}\endmoddef
%%BeginProcSet: aplotdict 1.0 0
%
/aplot 120 dict def aplot begin
/min \{ 2 copy gt \{ exch \} if pop \} bdf 
/max \{ 2 copy lt \{ exch \} if pop \} bdf
/Xscm \{ Xscale mul \} bdf /Xscme \{ Xscm exch \} bdf
/Yscm \{ Yscale mul \} bdf /Yscme \{ Yscm exch \} bdf
/fmt \{ Yscme Xscme m \} bdf /flt \{ Yscme Xscme l \} bdf
/line \{ scmyk slw m l K \} bdf
/uline \{
  scmyk slw m S htag 1 eq \{ 0 -0.1 cm \} \{ 0.1 cm 0 \} ifelse
  rl K R l S htag 1 eq \{ 0 -0.1 cm \} \{ 0.1 cm 0 \} ifelse
  rl K R K
  \} bdf
/ZoomTicks \{
  /zmdict 3 dict def zmdict begin
  /r \{ TxWB BDspl mul Xscm \} def /s \{ TyWB BDspl mul Yscm \} def
  /corner \{ S 10 -2 roll m 
    2 \{ rl S BGcolor scmyk .4 slw K R rl
      S FGcolor scmyk 2 slw [1 3] 0 setdash K R
      \} repeat R 
    \} def
  4 copy 3 1 roll exch
  0 s 0 s neg r neg 0 r 0 corner
  0 s neg 0 s r 0 r neg 0 corner
  0 s neg 0 s r neg 0 r 0 corner
  0 s 0 s neg r 0 r neg 0 corner end
  \} def
/Line \{
  S 9 5 roll 
    2 \{ Yscm 4 1 roll Xscm 4 1 roll \} repeat
    9 4 roll line
  R \} bdf
/Xline \{ 
  S 3 1 roll Xscme Xscme 3 -1 roll Yscm xwdt sub dup
    3 1 roll xwdt 9 -4 roll line
  R \} bdf
/Bline \{
  S htag 1 eq \{ Xscme Xscme y0 Yscme y1 Yscm bbox \}
     \{ Yscme Yscme X0 Xscm 3 1 roll X1 Xscme bbox \} ifelse
  S scmyk fill 
  R scmyk slw K
  R \} bdf
/Bsquare \{
  S Yscme Yscme 4 2 roll Xscme Xscme 4 1 roll exch bbox 
  S scmyk fill 
  R scmyk slw K
  R \} bdf
/Msquare \{
  S Yscme Yscme 4 2 roll Xscme Xscme 4 1 roll exch bbox
    scmyk slw K
  R \} bdf
/Mcircle \{
  S Yscme Xscme 3 -1 roll Xscm 0 360 arc closepath scmyk slw K
  R \} bdf
/Join \{
  S 2 copy 2 copy pop sub 2 div add exch
    htag 1 eq \{
      y1 TyWB add dup dup TyWB 0.75 mul add 4 1 roll 5 1 roll
      \} \{
        X0 TxWB sub dup dup TxWB 0.75 mul sub 5 1 roll 6 1 roll exch
      \} ifelse
    3 \{ Yscme Xscme 6 2 roll \} repeat
    m l l 0.25 slw scmyk K
  R \} bdf
/Arrow \{
  /acol [ 9 -4 roll ] def /acolor \{ acol aload pop \} def
  S 1 eq \{ exch /sn \{ 1 mul \} def \} \{ /sn \{ 1 neg mul \} def \} ifelse
    htag 1 eq \{ Xscm dup y1 Yscm HWBox add m
      HWarw sn HWarw rl 0 Warw neg rl HWarw neg sn HWarw rl closepath
      S acolor scmyk fill R
      y1 Yscm HWBox add m Xscm y1 Yscm HWBox add l acolor scmyk 1 slw K
      \} \{ Yscm dup X0 Xscm HWBox sub exch m
        HWarw neg HWarw sn rl Warw 0 rl HWarw neg HWarw neg sn rl closepath
        S acolor scmyk fill R
        X0 Xscm HWBox sub exch m Yscm X0 Xscm HWBox sub exch l
        acolor scmyk 1 slw K
      \} ifelse
  R \} bdf
/FBox \{
  htag 1 eq \{
    Xscme Xscme y1 Yscme y1 TyWB FBDspl mul add Yscm bbox
    \} \{
      Yscme Yscme X0 Xscm 3 1 roll X0 TxWB FBDspl mul sub Xscme bbox
    \} ifelse
  S scmyk fill R FGcolor scmyk 1 slw K
  \} bdf
/FTalgn \{
  htag 1 eq \{
    FTXangle 0 eq \{ (bv) (ch) \} \{ (cv) (lh) \} ifelse
    \} \{
      FTYangle 0 eq \{ (cv) (rh) \} \{ (bv) (rh) \} ifelse
    \} ifelse
  \} bdf
/GPalgn \{
  htag 1 eq \{
    GPXangle 0 eq \{ (bv) (ch) \} \{ (cv) (lh) \} ifelse
    \} \{
      GPYangle 0 eq \{ (cv) (rh) \} \{ (bv) (rh) \} ifelse
    \} ifelse
  \} bdf
/Box \{
  2 copy 2 copy pop sub 2 div add 7 1 roll
  S htag 1 eq \{
    Xscme Xscme y1 Yscme y1 TyWB add Yscm bbox
    \} \{
      Yscme Yscme X0 Xscm 3 1 roll X0 TxWB sub Xscme bbox
    \} ifelse
  S scmyk fill R
  FGcolor scmyk 1 slw K
  htag 1 eq \{
    Xscm y1 TyWB 1.75 mul add Yscm FTXangle
    \} \{
      Yscm X0 TxWB 1.75 mul sub Xscme FTYangle
    \} ifelse
  6 -1 roll FTalgn 8 -2 roll FGcolor ttxt
  R \} bdf
%
/GDmore \{
  MxFtLBL S ElmFont sfont (M) stringwidth pop R mul
  htag 1 eq \{ FTXangle sin \} \{ FTYangle cos \} ifelse
  abs mul ivcm add
  \} bdf
/BDmore \{
  MxGpLBL S TagFont sfont (M) stringwidth pop R mul
  htag 1 eq \{ GPXangle sin \} \{ GPYangle cos \} ifelse
  abs mul ivcm add
  \} bdf
%
/GnBanner\{
  S 1 eq \{
      2 copy
      htag 1 eq \{
        Xscme Xscme y1 TyWB GDspl mul add dup Yscme Yscm 3 1 roll
        \} \{
          Yscme Yscme X0 TxWB GDspl mul sub dup Xscme Xscme 4 1 roll exch
        \} ifelse
      0.5 FGcolor uline
      \} if
    2 copy pop sub 2 div add
    htag 1 eq \{
      Xscm y1 TyWB GLDspl mul add Yscm GPXangle
      \} \{
        Yscm X0 TxWB GLDspl mul sub Xscme GPYangle
      \} ifelse
    6 -1 roll GPalgn 8 -2 roll FGcolor ttxt
  R \} bdf
/SbBanner \{
  S htag 1 eq \{
      0 X0 X1 X0 sub 2 div add Xscm y1 TyWB GDspl mul add Yscm
      \} \{
        90 X0 TxWB GDspl mul sub Xscm y0 y1 y0 sub 2 div add Yscm
      \} ifelse
    5 -2 roll FGcolor ctshow
  R \} bdf
/Banner \{
  S htag 1 eq \{
      0 X0 X1 X0 sub 2 div add Xscm y1 TyWB BDspl mul add Yscm
      \} \{
        90 X0 TxWB BDspl mul sub Xscm y0 y1 y0 sub 2 div add Yscm
      \} ifelse
    5 -2 roll FGcolor ctshow
  R \} bdf
%
% mxt mnt xp yp ori end htick
/tckdict 15 dict def
 tckdict begin
 /mkmxt \{
  dup 0 lt \{ neg \} if
  dup 10 lt \{
    10 mul log round 10 exch exp cvi
    \} \{
      log round 10 exch exp cvi
    \} ifelse
  \} def
 /nwmod \{
  dup 1 le \{
    100 mul cvi exch 100 mul cvi exch mod 100 div
    \} \{
      exch dup
      1 le \{
        100 mul cvi exch 100 mul cvi mod 100 div
        \} \{
          cvi exch cvi mod
        \} ifelse
    \} ifelse
  \} def
 /isltone \{ dup 1 lt \{ 100 mul cvi 100 div \} if \} def
end
/htick \{ 
  S tckdict begin horizontal 
    /yp exch Yscm def /xp exch Xscm def /xend xdf /xori xdf
    /nmnt exch cvi def /nmxt exch cvi def
    /mxt exch dup 0 lt \{ pop xend xori sub mkmxt \} if def
    /mnt exch dup 0 lt \{ pop mxt nmnt div \} if def
    /lori xori dup mnt nwmod sub mnt add def
    /lend xend dup mnt nwmod sub mnt sub def
    xp yp T
    lori mnt lend \{
      isltone dup dup xori gt exch xend lt and \{
        dup Xscm 0 m dup dup Xscme
        mxt nwmod 0 eq \{ 7.5 \} \{ 4 \} ifelse neg l
        1 slw FGcolor scmyk K
        GridON 1 eq \{
          S 0 y0 Yscm neg T dup Xscm dup y0 Yscm m y1 Yscm l
          0.1 slw verylightgrey scmyk K R
          \} if
        dup mxt nwmod 0 eq \{
          dup xend mnt sub exch ge \{
            dup dup 1 ge \{ cvi \} if
            10 string cvs 0 3 -1 roll Xscm -18 TickFont FGcolor ctshow
            \} if
          \} \{
            pop
          \} ifelse
        \} if
      \} for
    xori Xscm dup 0 m 7.5 neg l 2 slw FGcolor scmyk K
    xori 10 string cvs 0 xori Xscm ZoomON 1 eq \{ 4 sub \} if
    -18 TickFont FGcolor ZoomON 0 eq \{ ctshow \} \{ ltshow \} ifelse
    xend Xscm dup 0 m 7.5 neg l 2 slw FGcolor scmyk K
    xend 10 string cvs 0 xend Xscm ZoomON 1 eq \{ 4 add \} if
    -18 TickFont FGcolor ZoomON 0 eq \{ ctshow \} \{ tshow \} ifelse
  end R \} def
/vtick \{
  S tckdict begin vertical
    /yp exch Yscm def /xp exch Xscm def /xend xdf /xori xdf
    /nmnt exch cvi def /nmxt exch cvi def
    /mxt exch dup 0 lt \{ pop xend xori sub mkmxt \} if def
    /mnt exch dup 0 lt \{ pop mxt nmnt div \} if def
    /lori xori dup mnt nwmod sub mnt add def
    /lend xend dup mnt nwmod sub mnt sub def
    xp yp T
    lori mnt lend \{
      isltone dup dup xori gt exch xend lt and \{
        dup Yscm 0 exch m dup dup Yscme
        mxt nwmod 0 eq \{ 7.5 \} \{ 4 \} ifelse exch l
        1 slw FGcolor scmyk K
        GridON 1 eq \{
          S X0 Xscm 0 T dup Yscm dup X0 neg Xscme m
          X1 neg Xscme l 0.1 slw verylightgrey scmyk K R
          \} if
        dup 0 eq \{
          S dup dup X0 Xscme Yscm m X1 neg Xscme Yscm l
          0.1 slw FGcolor scmyk K R
          \} if
        dup mxt nwmod 0 eq \{
          dup xend mnt sub exch ge \{
            dup dup 1 ge \{ cvi \} if
            10 string cvs 0 10 4 -1 roll Yscm 2.5 sub TickFont FGcolor tshow
            \} if
          \} \{
            pop
          \} ifelse
        \} if
      \} for
    7.5 xori Yscm dup 0 exch m l 2 slw FGcolor scmyk K
    xori 10 string cvs 0 10 xori Yscm
    ZoomON 0 eq \{ 2.5 sub \} \{ 2.5 add \} ifelse
    TickFont FGcolor tshow 7.5 xend Yscm dup 0 exch m l
    2 slw FGcolor scmyk K xend 10 string cvs 0 10 xend Yscm
    ZoomON 0 eq \{ 2.5 sub \} \{ 2.5 add \} ifelse
    TickFont FGcolor tshow end
  R \} def
/nucltick \{ tickmn tickmx maxtck mintck X0 X1 0 y0 htick \} def
/pctmarks \{
  S y0 10 y1 \{
      Yscm dup X0 Xscm X1 Xscm 3 1 roll 4 1 roll 0.5 FGcolor line
      \} for
  R \} bdf
%
/beginfunct \{
  R S 3 dict begin
    /maxx exch ceiling def /minx exch floor def
    /Yscale XBoxY maxx minx sub div def
    minx 0 lt \{ 0 minx neg Yscm T \} if
    S XBYtickflg 1 eq \{
        -1 -1 xtrmxt xtrmnt minx maxx X1 0 vtick
        S X0 Xscm 0 m X1 Xscm 0 l dotted FGcolor scmyk K R
        \} if
    R
  \} def /endfunct \{ end R \} def
end % aplot dict
%
%%EndProcSet:   aplotdict 1.0 0
%
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-PosF.3-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{636}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{Main functions definition}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{637}\sublabel{NWgff18-POSU-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSU-1}}}\moddef{POSTSCRIPT main function calls~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-POSU-1}}}\endmoddef
%%BeginProcSet: main_function_calls 1.0 0
%
/s_credits \{
  S 1 dict begin
    /fs_cd FSF def
    pagedict begin
    pga4 pop end 1 cm sub DnM T 0 0 0
(This plot has been obtained using GFF2APLOT. The most recent version of GFF2APLOT is freely available at \\042http:\\/\\/www1.imim.es/software/gfftools/APLOT.html\\042. Copyright      1999 by Josep F. ABRIL, Thomas WIEHE & Roderic GUIGO)
    (cv) (rh) fs_cd /Times-Roman FGcolor ttxt
    S fs_cd /Times-Roman sfont
    (   1999 by Josep F. ABRIL, Thomas WIEHE & Roderic GUIGO)
    stringwidth pop neg R 0 0 (\\343) (cv) (ch) fs_cd /Symbol FGcolor ttxt
    end
  R \} bdf
%
/estlbl \{
  S 3 dict begin
    /lbl xdf /ypos xdf /xpos xdf
    horizontal
      0 Xlwdt 4 div neg T
      lbl 0 xpos Xscm ypos Yscm 5 /Helvetica black ctshow
    vertical
    end
  R \} bdf
%
/GsclonX \{
  /Y exch Y Spacer sub exch sub def
  Xmarg Y T
  axesp 0 eq \{
    /Xscale \{ BBoxX X1 X0 sub Y1 Y0 sub max div \} def
    \} \{
      /Xscale \{ BBoxX X1 X0 sub div \} def
    \} ifelse
  \} bdf
%
% DOTPLOT BOX
/begindata \{
 aplot begin
  S /y1 Y1 def /y0 Y0 def
    BBoxY GsclonX
    axesp 0 eq \{
      /Yscale Xscale def
      \} \{
        /Yscale \{ BBoxY y1 y0 sub div \} def
      \} ifelse
    /TxWB \{ WBox Xscale div \} def /TyWB \{ WBox Yscale div \} def
    /GDspl \{ xGDspl GDmore \} def /GLDspl \{ xGLDspl GDmore \} def
    /BDspl \{ xBDspl GDmore BDmore \} def
    X0 Xscm neg y0 Yscm neg T
    S X0 Xscm y0 Yscm X1 Xscm y1 Yscm bbox BBoxcol scmyk fill R
    S X0 Xscm y0 Yscm X1 Xscm y1 Yscm
      ZoomON 1 eq \{ 4 copy ZoomTicks \} if bbox
      2 slw FGcolor scmyk K
    R
    S BBXtickflg 1 eq \{
        nucltick /Spacer 1 cm def
        \} \{
          /Spacer 0.5 cm def
        \} ifelse
      BBYtickflg 1 eq \{
        tickmn tickmx maxtck mintck y0 y1 X1 0 vtick
        \} if
    R newpath
 \} def
/enddata \{ R /GDspl xGDspl def /GLDspl xGLDspl def /BDspl xBDspl def end \} def
%
% PERCENT BOX
/beginmatches \{
 aplot begin 
   /ZoomON 0 def S /y1 xdf /y0 xdf SBoxY GsclonX
   /Yscale SBoxY y1 y0 sub div def
   X0 Xscm neg y0 Yscm neg T S X0 Xscm y0 Yscm X1 Xscm y1 Yscm bbox
   S
     S SBoxcol scmyk fill R
     S SBoxLab TagLabelFont Banner SBoxSLab TagFont SbBanner
       SBXtickflg 1 eq \{
         nucltick /Spacer 1 cm def
         \} \{
           /Spacer 0.5 cm def
         \} ifelse
     R
     S SBYtickflg 1 eq \{ -1 -1 pctmxt pctmnt y0 y1 X1 0 vtick \} if
     R
     S X0 Xscm y0 Yscm X1 Xscm y1 Yscm bbox 2 slw FGcolor scmyk K
     R
   R clip newpath
 \} def /endmatches \{ R R end \} def
%
% EXTRA BOX
/beginextra \{
 aplot begin
   S /nlines xdf /y0 0 def XBoxY GsclonX
     /Yscale XBoxY nlines 1 add div def
     /Xlwdt Yscale 0.75 mul def /xwdt Yscale 2 div def
     /y1 XBoxY Yscale div def
     X0 Xscm neg 0 T
     S X0 Xscm y0 Yscm X1 Xscm y1 Yscm bbox
       S XBoxcol scmyk fill R
       S XBoxLab TagLabelFont Banner XBoxSLab TagFont SbBanner
         XBXtickflg 1 eq \{ nucltick \} if
       R newpath
  \} def
/endextra \{
  /Yscale XBoxY nlines 1 add div def
  X0 Xscm y0 Yscm X1 Xscm y1 Yscm bbox
  2 slw FGcolor scmyk K R
  R end
  \} def

\nwused{\\{NWgff18-PosF.3-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{638}\nwdocspar

\sctn{Reporting Program Execution} %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\subsctn{Signal trapping}

In this version of {\prog} we are trapping signals, to exit from this program but reporting that was a user action, not a program error. We will close '{\tt{}LOGFILE}' if opened. 

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{639}\sublabel{NWgff18-TraG-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-TraG-1}}}\moddef{Trapping signals~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-TraG-1}}}\endmoddef
$SIG\{HUP\}  = \\&trap_signals_prog;
$SIG\{ABRT\} = \\&trap_signals;
$SIG\{INT\}  = \\&trap_signals;
$SIG\{QUIT\} = \\&trap_signals;
$SIG\{TERM\} = \\&trap_signals;
$SIG\{KILL\} = \\&trap_signals;
$SIG\{CHLD\} = 'IGNORE';
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-UseB-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{640}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{641}\sublabel{NWgff18-ComF-2}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-2}}}\moddef{Common Routines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-1}}}\plusendmoddef
sub trap_signals() \{
    &prt_to_logfile($ErrorList\{'USER_HALT'\});
    &close_logfile();
    die($ErrorList\{'USER_HALT'\});
\}
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{642}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{643}\sublabel{NWgff18-ComF-3}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-3}}}\moddef{Common Routines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-1}}}\plusendmoddef
sub trap_signals_prog() \{
    &prt_to_logfile($ErrorList\{'PROCESS_HALT'\});
    &close_logfile();
    die($ErrorList\{'PROCESS_HALT'\});
\}
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{644}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{645}\sublabel{NWgff18-outN-2}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-outN-2}}}\moddef{warnings - input/output~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-outN-1}}}\plusendmoddef
USER_HALT =>
  $spl.$Warn."$PROGRAM has been stopped by user !!!\\n".
  $spl.$Warn."---------- Exiting NOW !!! ----------\\n".$spl,
PROCESS_HALT =>
  $spl.$Warn."------- $PROGRAM is down !!! -------\\n".
  $spl.$Warn."---------- Exiting NOW !!! ----------\\n".$spl,
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{646}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{Dumping complex data structures}

With '{\tt{}Data::Dumper}' we are able to pretty print complex data structures for debugging them. We include also a command-line switch to enable this feature, but it requires a log file definition with '{\tt{}-V}' option.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{647}\sublabel{NWgff18-UseB-3}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-UseB-3}}}\moddef{Use Modules~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-UseB-1}}}\plusendmoddef
use Data::Dumper;
local $Data::Dumper::Purity = 0;
local $Data::Dumper::Deepcopy = 1;
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{648}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{649}\sublabel{NWgff18-perI-3}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-perI-3}}}\moddef{perl requires help~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-perI-1}}}\plusendmoddef
"Data::Dumper" - pretty printing data structures for debugging (*).
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{650}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{651}\sublabel{NWgff18-comK-Y}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-comK-Y}}}\moddef{command-line options~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-comK-1}}}\plusendmoddef
"debug"  => \\$Debug, # Dumps Vars -> LogFile
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{652}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{653}\sublabel{NWgff18-comH-Z}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-comH-Z}}}\moddef{command-line help~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-comH-1}}}\plusendmoddef
-debug    Reporting variable contents when testing the program.
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{654}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{Reporting errors and warnings}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{655}\sublabel{NWgff18-GloG-5}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloG-5}}}\moddef{Global Constants~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloG-1}}}\plusendmoddef
my $Error = "\\<\\<\\<  ERROR  \\>\\>\\> ";
my $Warn  = "\\<\\<\\< WARNING \\>\\>\\> ";
my $spl   = "\\<\\<\\<\\-\\-\\-\\-\\-\\-\\-\\-\\-\\>\\>\\>\\n";
my $spw   = "\\<\\<\\<         \\>\\>\\> ";
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{656}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{657}\sublabel{NWgff18-GloB-G}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-G}}}\moddef{Global Vars~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-1}}}\plusendmoddef
#
# Error/Warning Message List
my %ErrorList = (
                 \LA{}warnings - input/output~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-outN-1}}\RA{}
                 \LA{}warnings - parsing command-line options~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ward-1}}\RA{}
                 \LA{}warnings - parsing custom files~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-warV-1}}\RA{}
                 \LA{}warnings - parsing GFF files~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-warS-1}}\RA{}
                 );
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{658}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{659}\sublabel{NWgff18-ComF-4}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-4}}}\moddef{Common Routines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-1}}}\plusendmoddef
sub warn() \{
    my $type = shift @_;
    my $screen_flg = shift @_;
    my $comment = sprintf($ErrorList\{$type\}, @_);
    # ALWAYS to STDERR if $screen_flg==$T unless $Quiet==$T
    $screen_flg && ($Quiet || print STDERR $comment); 
    &prt_to_logfile($comment);
\} # warn
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{660}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{661}\sublabel{NWgff18-ComF-5}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-5}}}\moddef{Common Routines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-1}}}\plusendmoddef
sub prt_to_logfile() \{ $LogFile && (print LOGFILE $_[0]) \}
sub prt_to_stderr()  \{ $Verbose && ($Quiet || print STDERR $_[0]) \}
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{662}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{Reporting messages}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{663}\sublabel{NWgff18-GloG-6}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloG-6}}}\moddef{Global Constants~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloG-1}}}\plusendmoddef
my $line = ("#" x 80)."\\n";
my $sp = "###\\n";
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{664}\nwdocspar
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{665}\sublabel{NWgff18-GloB-H}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-H}}}\moddef{Global Vars~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-1}}}\plusendmoddef
#
# Verbose Message List
my %MessageList = (
                   \LA{}messages - input/output~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-outN.2-1}}\RA{}
                   \LA{}messages - parsing command-line options~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-mesd-1}}\RA{}
                   \LA{}messages - parsing custom files~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-mesV-1}}\RA{}
                   \LA{}messages - parsing GFF files~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-mesS-1}}\RA{}
                   );
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{666}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{667}\sublabel{NWgff18-ComF-6}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-6}}}\moddef{Common Routines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-1}}}\plusendmoddef
sub report() \{
    my $type = shift @_;
    my $comment = sprintf($MessageList\{$type\},@_);
    &prt_to_stderr($comment);
    &prt_to_logfile($comment);
\} # report
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{668}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{669}\sublabel{NWgff18-ComF-7}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-7}}}\moddef{Common Routines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-1}}}\plusendmoddef
sub header() \{
    my $comment = $line;
    foreach my $ln (@_) \{ 
        $comment .= "### ".&fill_mid("$ln",72," ")." ###\\n";
        \};
    $comment .= $line;
    &prt_to_stderr($comment);
    &prt_to_logfile($comment);
\} # header
sub footer() \{
    $total_time = &timing($F);
    &header(@_,$total_time);
    &prt_to_stderr("###\\n");
    &prt_to_logfile("###\\n");
\}
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{670}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{Timing procedures}

The '{\tt{}Benchmark}' module encapsulates a number of routines to help to figure out how long it takes to execute a piece of code and the whole script.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{671}\sublabel{NWgff18-UseB-4}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-UseB-4}}}\moddef{Use Modules~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-UseB-1}}}\plusendmoddef
use Benchmark;
  \LA{}Timer ON~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-Tim8-1}}\RA{}
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{672}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{673}\sublabel{NWgff18-perI-4}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-perI-4}}}\moddef{perl requires help~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-perI-1}}}\plusendmoddef
"Benchmark" - checking and comparing running times of code.
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{674}\nwdocspar

See '{\tt{}man\ Benchmark}' for further info about this package. 
We set an array to keep record of timing for each section.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{675}\sublabel{NWgff18-Tim8-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-Tim8-1}}}\moddef{Timer ON~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-Tim8-1}}}\endmoddef
my @Timer = (new Benchmark);
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-UseB-4}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{676}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{677}\sublabel{NWgff18-ComF-8}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-8}}}\moddef{Common Routines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-1}}}\plusendmoddef
sub timing() \{
    push @Timer, (new Benchmark);
    # partial time 
    $_[0] || 
        (return timestr(timediff($Timer[$#Timer],$Timer[($#Timer - 1)])));
    # total time
    return timestr(timediff($Timer[$#Timer],$Timer[0]));
\}
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{678}\nwdocspar

We also set here the date when the script is running and who is the user running it.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{679}\sublabel{NWgff18-GloB-I}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-I}}}\moddef{Global Vars~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GloB-1}}}\plusendmoddef
my $total_time = 0;
my $DATE = localtime;
my $USER = $ENV\{USER\};
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{680}\nwdocspar

\sctn{Common code blocks} %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\subsctn{PERL scripts}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{697}\sublabel{NWgff18-PERC-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PERC-1}}}\moddef{PERL shebang~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PERC-1}}}\endmoddef
#!/usr/bin/perl -w
# This is perl, version 5.005_03 built for i386-linux
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-APL5-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{698}\nwdocspar

The 'shebang' line can be emulated in several ways. Those systems that do not support '{\tt{}{\char35}!}' will emulate it with:

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{699}\sublabel{NWgff18-PERM-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PERM-1}}}\moddef{PERL shebang emulation~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PERM-1}}}\endmoddef
#!/usr/bin/perl -w
eval 'exec /usr/bin/perl -w -S $0 $\{1+"$@"\}' if $running_under_some_shell;
\nwnotused{PERL\ shebang\ emulation}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{700}\nwdocspar

Another way to emulate the 'shebang' line is the following devious construct that will work under any of csh, sh, or perl system.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{701}\sublabel{NWgff18-PERU-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PERU-1}}}\moddef{PERL shebang general emulation~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-PERU-1}}}\endmoddef
eval '\{exit $?0\}' && 
  eval 'exec /usr/bin/perl -w -S $0 $\{1+"$@"\}' &&
    eval 'exec /usr/bin/perl -w -S $0 $argv:q' 
      if 0;
\nwnotused{PERL\ shebang\ general\ emulation}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{702}\nwdocspar

We also include a copy of the GNU-GPL as a comment at first lines on the program, and the version control tag.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{703}\sublabel{NWgff18-ProC-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ProC-1}}}\moddef{Program Info~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ProC-1}}}\endmoddef
#
\LA{}GNU License PERL~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-GNUG-1}}\RA{}
#
\LA{}Version Control Id Tag~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-VerM-1}}\RA{}
#
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-APL5-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{704}\nwdocspar

We are using here {\tt{}perl\ -w} to show all warnings when running the script. We also {\tt{}use\ strict} to force all variable names to be declared.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{705}\sublabel{NWgff18-SkiV-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-SkiV-1}}}\moddef{Skip comments and empty records~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-SkiV-1}}}\endmoddef
next if /^\\#/o;
next if /^\\s*$/o;
chomp;
\nwnotused{Skip\ comments\ and\ empty\ records}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{706}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{707}\sublabel{NWgff18-ComF-9}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-9}}}\moddef{Common Routines~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-ComF-1}}}\plusendmoddef
#
sub max() \{
    my $z = shift @_;
    foreach my $l (@_) \{ $z = $l if $l > $z \};
    return $z;
\} # max
sub min() \{
    my $z = shift @_;
    foreach my $l (@_) \{ $z = $l if $l < $z \};
    return $z;
\} # min
#
sub fill_right() \{ $_[0].($_[2] x ($_[1] - length($_[0]))) \}
sub fill_left()  \{ ($_[2] x ($_[1] - length($_[0]))).$_[0] \}
sub fill_mid()   \{ 
    my $l = length($_[0]);
    my $k = int(($_[1] - $l)/2);
    ($_[2] x $k).$_[0].($_[2] x ($_[1] - ($l+$k)));
\} # fill_mid
#
sub counter \{ # $_[0]~current_pos++ $_[1]~char
    print STDERR "$_[1]";
    (($_[0] % 50) == 0) && (print STDERR "[".&fill_left($_[0],6,"0")."]\\n");
\} # counter
#
sub counter_end \{ # $_[0]~current_pos   $_[1]~char
    (($_[0] % 50) != 0) && (print STDERR "[".&fill_left($_[0],6,"0")."]\\n");
\} # counter_end
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{708}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{BASH scripts}

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{709}\sublabel{NWgff18-BASC-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASC-1}}}\moddef{BASH shebang~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASC-1}}}\endmoddef
#!/usr/bin/bash
# GNU bash, version 2.03.6(1)-release (i386-redhat-linux-gnu)
\LA{}Version Control Id Tag~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-VerM-1}}\RA{}
#
SECONDS=0 # Reset Timing
# Which script are we running...
L="####################"
\{ echo "$L$L$L$L";
  echo "### RUNNING [$0]";
  echo "### Current date:`date`";
  echo "###"; \} 1>&2;
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-wea7-1}\\{NWgff18-LaT8-1}\\{NWgff18-TheA-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{710}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{711}\sublabel{NWgff18-BASJ-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASJ-1}}}\moddef{BASH script closure~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASJ-1}}}\endmoddef
\{ echo "###"; echo "### Execution time for [$0] : $SECONDS secs";
  echo "$L$L$L$L";
  echo ""; \} 1>&2;
#
exit 0
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-wea7-1}\\{NWgff18-LaT8-1}\\{NWgff18-TheA-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{712}\nwdocspar

\sctn{Extracting code blocks from this document} %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

From this file we can obtain both the code and the
documentation. The following instructions are needed:

\subsctn{Extracting Script code chunks from the {\tt{}noweb} file} % \\[-0.5ex]

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{719}\sublabel{NWgff18-tan8-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tan8-1}}}\moddef{tangling~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tan8-1}}}\endmoddef
# showing line numbering comments in program
notangle -L -R"APLOT" $WORK/$nwfile.nw | \\
    perl -ne '$.>1 && print' - > $BIN/gff2aplot.pl ;
chmod a+x $BIN/gff2aplot.pl ;
#
\nwalsodefined{\\{NWgff18-tan8-2}\\{NWgff18-tan8-3}\\{NWgff18-tan8-4}\\{NWgff18-tan8-5}}\nwnotused{tangling}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{720}\nwdocspar
 
\begin{comment}
\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{721}\sublabel{NWgff18-newE-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-newE-1}}}\moddef{new LaTeX urls~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-newE-1}}}\endmoddef
\\def\\perltidy\{
 \\htmladdnormallinkfoot\{\\texttt\{perltidy\}\}
                   \{\\url|http://perltidy.sourceforge.net/|\}
 \} % def perltidy
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-LaTS-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{722}\nwdocspar
\end{comment}
We use {\perltidy} to reformat final versions of perl scripts (without line numbering comments, correct indentations, etc...) and to pretty-print in html format.

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{723}\sublabel{NWgff18-tan8-2}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tan8-2}}}\moddef{tangling~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tan8-1}}}\plusendmoddef
# reformating program with perltidy
notangle -R"APLOT" $WORK/$nwfile.nw | \\
    perltidy - > $BIN/$nwfile.pl ;
# pretty-printing program with perltidy
notangle -R"APLOT" $WORK/$nwfile.nw | \\
    perltidy -html - > $DOCS/html/$nwfile.html ;
#
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{724}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{Extracting different Config Files} % \\[-0.5ex]

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{725}\sublabel{NWgff18-tan8-3}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tan8-3}}}\moddef{tangling~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tan8-1}}}\plusendmoddef
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{726}\nwdocspar

\subsctn{Extracting documentation and \LaTeX{}'ing it} % \\[-0.5ex] %'

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{727}\sublabel{NWgff18-tan8-4}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tan8-4}}}\moddef{tangling~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tan8-1}}}\plusendmoddef
# extracting main document processors
notangle -R"weaving"    $WORK/$nwfile.nw > $WORK/nw2tex ;
notangle -R"LaTeXing"   $WORK/$nwfile.nw > $WORK/ltx ;
notangle -R"The Manual" $WORK/$nwfile.nw > $WORK/mkdoc ;
#
\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{728}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{729}\sublabel{NWgff18-tanY-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tanY-1}}}\moddef{tangling complementary LaTeX files~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tanY-1}}}\endmoddef
# extracting complementary material 
echo "Extracting \\"$DOCS/defs.tex\\"..." ;
notangle -R"LaTeX deploy new definitions" $WORK/$nwfile.nw \\
         > $DOCS/defs.tex ;
echo "Extracting \\"$DOCS/AplotCLoptions.tex\\"..." ;
notangle -R"LATEX command-line" $WORK/$nwfile.nw \\
         > $DOCS/tables/AplotCLoptions.tex ;
echo "Extracting \\"$DOCS/AplotCLoptionsTbl.tex\\"..." ;
notangle -R"LATEX command-line table" $WORK/$nwfile.nw \\
         > $DOCS/tables/AplotCLoptionsTbl.tex ;
echo "Extracting \\"$DOCS/AplotCustomVars.tex\\"..." ;
notangle -R"LATEX custom-vars" $WORK/$nwfile.nw  \\
         > $DOCS/tables/AplotCustomVars.tex ;
echo "Extracting \\"$DOCS/AplotCustomVarsTbl.tex\\"..." ;
notangle -R"LATEX custom-vars table" $WORK/$nwfile.nw  \\
         > $DOCS/tables/AplotCustomVarsTbl.tex ;
echo "Extracting \\"$DOCS/AplotColorDefs.tex\\"..." ;
notangle -R"LATEX cmyk colors" $WORK/$nwfile.nw  \\
         > $DOCS/tables/AplotColorDefs.tex ;
echo "Extracting \\"$DOCS/AplotColorTbl.tex\\"..." ;
notangle -R"LATEX colors table" $WORK/$nwfile.nw  \\
         > $DOCS/tables/AplotColorTbl.tex ;
echo "Extracting \\"$DOCS/AplotPageSizeTbl.tex\\"..." ;
notangle -R"LATEX page format table" $WORK/$nwfile.nw \\
         > $DOCS/tables/AplotPageSizeTbl.tex ;
echo "Extracting \\"$DOCS/DataStructure_GFF.tex\\"..." ;
notangle -R"GFF DATA STRUCTURE" $WORK/$nwfile.nw \\
         > $DOCS/tables/DataStructure_GFF.tex ;
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-wea7-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{730}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{731}\sublabel{NWgff18-wea7-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-wea7-1}}}\moddef{weaving~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-wea7-1}}}\endmoddef
\LA{}BASH shebang~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASC-1}}\RA{}
# weaving and LaTeXing
\LA{}BASH Environment Variables~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASQ-1}}\RA{}
\LA{}tangling complementary LaTeX files~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tanY-1}}\RA{}
# extracting main documentation
echo "Weaving \\"$DOCS/$nwfile.tex\\"..." ;
noweave -t4 -delay -x $WORK/$nwfile.nw > $DOCS/$nwfile.tex ;
# LaTeXing 
echo "LaTeXing \\"$DOCS/$nwfile.tex\\"..." ;
pushd $DOCS/ ;
latex $nwfile.tex ;
dvips $nwfile.dvi -o $nwfile.ps -t a4 ;
popd;
\LA{}BASH script closure~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASJ-1}}\RA{}
\nwnotused{weaving}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{732}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{733}\sublabel{NWgff18-LaT8-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-LaT8-1}}}\moddef{LaTeXing~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-LaT8-1}}}\endmoddef
\LA{}BASH shebang~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASC-1}}\RA{}
# only LaTeXing
\LA{}BASH Environment Variables~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASQ-1}}\RA{}
pushd $DOCS/ ;
latex $nwfile.tex ; 
latex $nwfile.tex ; 
latex $nwfile.tex ;
dvips $nwfile.dvi -o $nwfile.ps -t a4 ;
pdflatex $nwfile.tex ;
popd ;
\LA{}BASH script closure~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASJ-1}}\RA{}
\nwnotused{LaTeXing}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{734}%$

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{735}\sublabel{NWgff18-TheA-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-TheA-1}}}\moddef{The Manual~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-TheA-1}}}\endmoddef
\LA{}BASH shebang~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASC-1}}\RA{}
# only LaTeXing
\LA{}BASH Environment Variables~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASQ-1}}\RA{}
MANUAL="GFF2APLOT_MANUAL";
pushd $DOCS/ ;
latex $MANUAL.tex ; 
latex $MANUAL.tex ; 
latex $MANUAL.tex ;
dvips $MANUAL.dvi -o $MANUAL.ps -t a4 ;
popd ;
\LA{}BASH script closure~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASJ-1}}\RA{}
\nwnotused{The\ Manual}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{736}%$

\subsctn{Defining working shell variables for the current project} % \\[-0.5ex]

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{737}\sublabel{NWgff18-BASQ-1}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASQ-1}}}\moddef{BASH Environment Variables~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-BASQ-1}}}\endmoddef
# Global Variables
WORK="$HOME/development/softjabril/gfftools/gff2aplot" ;
BIN="$WORK/bin" ;
PARAM="$BIN/param" ;
DOCS="$WORK/docs" ;
DATA="$WORK/data" ;
TEST="$WORK/tests" ;
nwfile="gff2aplot" ;
export WORK BIN PARAM DOCS DATA TEST nwfile ;
\nwused{\\{NWgff18-wea7-1}\\{NWgff18-LaT8-1}\\{NWgff18-TheA-1}}\nwendcode{}\nwbegindocs{738}\nwdocspar

\nwenddocs{}\nwbegincode{739}\sublabel{NWgff18-tan8-5}\nwmargintag{{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tan8-5}}}\moddef{tangling~{\nwtagstyle{}\subpageref{NWgff18-tan8-1}}}\plusendmoddef
#
# BASH Environment Variables
notangle -R'BASH Environment Variables' $WORK/$nwfile.nw \\
         > $WORK/.bash_VARS ; 
source $WORK/.bash_VARS ;
#
